SELECT MIN(chn.name) AS uncredited_voiced_character,        MIN(t.title) AS russian_movie FROM char_name AS chn,      cast_info AS ci,      company_name AS cn,      company_type AS ct,      movie_companies AS mc,      role_type AS rt,      title AS t WHERE ci.note LIKE '%(voice)%'   AND ci.note LIKE '%(uncredited)%'   AND cn.country_code = '[ru]'   AND rt.role = 'actor'   AND t.production_year > 2005   AND t.id = mc.movie_id   AND t.id = ci.movie_id   AND ci.movie_id = mc.movie_id   AND chn.id = ci.person_role_id   AND rt.id = ci.role_id   AND cn.id = mc.company_id   AND ct.id = mc.company_type_id
SELECT min(name_8) AS uncredited_voiced_character, min(title_38) AS russian_movie FROM (SELECT t10.name_8, t0.title_38 FROM (SELECT t9.name_8, t9.movie_id_16, t9.movie_id_31 FROM (SELECT t8.name_8, t8.movie_id_16, t8.role_id_20, t8.movie_id_31 FROM (SELECT t7.name_8, t7.movie_id_16, t7.role_id_20, t4.movie_id_31, t4.company_type_id_33 FROM (SELECT t6.name_8, t5.movie_id_16, t5.role_id_20 FROM (SELECT id AS id_7, name AS name_8 FROM char_name WHERE (id IS NOT NULL)) AS t6 INNER JOIN (SELECT movie_id AS movie_id_16, person_role_id AS person_role_id_17, role_id AS role_id_20 FROM cast_info WHERE (((note IS NOT NULL) AND ((note LIKE '%(voice)%') AND (note LIKE '%(uncredited)%'))) AND (((person_role_id IS NOT NULL) AND (movie_id IS NOT NULL)) AND (role_id IS NOT NULL)))) AS t5 ON (t6.id_7 = t5.person_role_id_17)) AS t7 INNER JOIN (SELECT movie_id AS movie_id_31, company_id AS company_id_32, company_type_id AS company_type_id_33 FROM movie_companies WHERE (((movie_id IS NOT NULL) AND (company_id IS NOT NULL)) AND (company_type_id IS NOT NULL))) AS t4 ON (t7.movie_id_16 = t4.movie_id_31) INNER JOIN (SELECT id AS id_21 FROM company_name WHERE (((country_code IS NOT NULL) AND (country_code = '[ru]')) AND (id IS NOT NULL))) AS t3 ON (t3.id_21 = t4.company_id_32)) AS t8 INNER JOIN (SELECT id AS id_28 FROM company_type WHERE (id IS NOT NULL)) AS t2 ON (t2.id_28 = t8.company_type_id_33)) AS t9 INNER JOIN (SELECT id AS id_35 FROM role_type WHERE (((role IS NOT NULL) AND (role = 'actor')) AND (id IS NOT NULL))) AS t1 ON (t1.id_35 = t9.role_id_20)) AS t10 INNER JOIN (SELECT id AS id_37, title AS title_38 FROM title WHERE (((production_year IS NOT NULL) AND (production_year > 2005)) AND (id IS NOT NULL))) AS t0 ON ((t0.id_37 = t10.movie_id_31) AND (t0.id_37 = t10.movie_id_16))) AS t11

t10.movie_id_28, t2.movie_id_31, link FROM ( SELECT t9.name_9, t9.movie_id_23, t4.movie_id_28 FROM ( SELECT t8.name_9, t8.movie_id_23 FROM ( SELECT t7.name_9, t6.movie_id_23, t6.company_type_id_25 FROM ( SELECT id AS id_8, name AS name_9 FROM company_name WHERE ( ( (country_code IS NOT NULL) AND ( NOT (country_code = '[pl]') AND ( (name LIKE '%Film%') OR (name LIKE '%Warner%') ) ) ) AND (id IS NOT NULL) ) ) AS t7 INNER JOIN ( SELECT movie_id AS movie_id_23, company_id AS company_id_24, company_type_id AS company_type_id_25 FROM movie_companies WHERE ( ( (note IS NULL) AND (company_id IS NOT NULL) ) AND ( (company_type_id IS NOT NULL) AND (movie_id IS NOT NULL) ) ) ) AS t6 ON (t6.company_id_24 = t7.id_8) ) AS t8 INNER JOIN ( SELECT id AS id_15 FROM company_type WHERE ( ( (kind IS NOT NULL) AND (kind = 'production companies') ) AND (id IS NOT NULL) ) ) AS t5 ON (t8.company_type_id_25 = t5.id_15) ) AS t9 INNER JOIN ( SELECT movie_id AS movie_id_28, keyword_id AS keyword_id_29 FROM movie_keyword WHERE ( (movie_id IS NOT NULL) AND (keyword_id IS NOT NULL) ) ) AS t4 ON (t4.movie_id_28 = t9.movie_id_23) INNER JOIN ( SELECT id AS id_17 FROM keyword WHERE ( ( (keyword IS NOT NULL) AND (keyword = 'sequel') ) AND (id IS NOT NULL) ) ) AS t3 ON (t4.keyword_id_29 = t3.id_17) ) AS t10 INNER JOIN ( SELECT movie_id AS movie_id_31, link_type_id AS link_type_id_33 FROM movie_link WHERE ( (movie_id IS NOT NULL) AND (link_type_id IS NOT NULL) ) ) AS t2 ON ( (t2.movie_id_31 = t10.movie_id_28) AND (t2.movie_id_31 = t10.movie_id_23) ) INNER JOIN ( SELECT * FROM link_type WHERE ( ( (link IS NOT NULL) AND (link LIKE '%follow%') ) AND (id IS NOT NULL) ) ) AS t1 ON (id = t2.link_type_id_33) ) AS t11 INNER JOIN ( SELECT id AS id_34, title AS title_35 FROM title WHERE ( ( (production_year IS NOT NULL) AND ( (production_year >= 1950) AND (production_year <= 2000) ) ) AND (id IS NOT NULL) ) ) AS t0 ON ( ( (t11.movie_id_31 = t0.id_34) AND (t0.id_34 = t11.movie_id_28) ) AND (t0.id_34 = t11.movie_id_23) ) ) AS t12

SELECT MIN(cn.name) AS movie_company,        MIN(mi_idx.info) AS rating,        MIN(t.title) AS drama_horror_movie FROM company_name AS cn,      company_type AS ct,      info_type AS it1,      info_type AS it2,      movie_companies AS mc,      movie_info AS mi,      movie_info_idx AS mi_idx,      title AS t WHERE cn.country_code = '[us]'   AND ct.kind = 'production companies'   AND it1.info = 'genres'   AND it2.info = 'rating'   AND mi.info IN ('Drama',                   'Horror')   AND mi_idx.info > '8.0'   AND t.production_year BETWEEN 2005 AND 2008   AND t.id = mi.movie_id   AND t.id = mi_idx.movie_id   AND mi.info_type_id = it1.id   AND mi_idx.info_type_id = it2.id   AND t.id = mc.movie_id   AND ct.id = mc.company_type_id   AND cn.id = mc.company_id   AND mc.movie_id = mi.movie_id   AND mc.movie_id = mi_idx.movie_id   AND mi.movie_id = mi_idx.movie_id
SELECT min(name_9) AS movie_company, min(info_34) AS rating, min(title_37) AS drama_horror_movie FROM (SELECT t11.name_9, t11.info_34, t0.title_37 FROM (SELECT t10.name_9, t10.movie_id_22, t10.movie_id_27, t2.movie_id_32, t2.info_34 FROM (SELECT t9.name_9, t9.movie_id_22, t4.movie_id_27 FROM (SELECT t8.name_9, t8.movie_id_22 FROM (SELECT t7.name_9, t6.movie_id_22, t6.company_type_id_24 FROM (SELECT id AS id_8, name AS name_9 FROM company_name WHERE (((country_code IS NOT NULL) AND (country_code = '[us]')) AND (id IS NOT NULL))) AS t7 INNER JOIN (SELECT movie_id AS movie_id_22, company_id AS company_id_23, company_type_id AS company_type_id_24 FROM movie_companies WHERE ((company_id IS NOT NULL) AND ((company_type_id IS NOT NULL) AND (movie_id IS NOT NULL)))) AS t6 ON (t7.id_8 = t6.company_id_23)) AS t8 INNER JOIN (SELECT id AS id_15 FROM company_type WHERE (((kind IS NOT NULL) AND (kind = 'production companies')) AND (id IS NOT NULL))) AS t5 ON (t5.id_15 = t9.movie_id_22, t9.info_24, t3.movie_id_27 FROM (SELECT t8.movie_id_17, t5.movie_id_22, t5.info_24 FROM (SELECT t6.movie_id_17 FROM (SELECT id AS id_7 FROM info_type WHERE (((info IS NOT NULL) AND (info = 'countries')) AND (id IS NOT NULL))) AS t7 INNER JOIN (SELECT movie_id AS movie_id_17, info_type_id AS info_type_id_18 FROM movie_info WHERE (info IN ('Sweden','Norway','Germany','Denmark','Swedish','Denish','Norwegian','German','USA','American') AND ((info_type_id IS NOT NULL) AND (movie_id IS NOT NULL)))) AS t6 ON (t7.id_7 = t6.info_type_id_18)) AS t8 INNER JOIN (SELECT movie_id AS movie_id_22, info_type_id AS info_type_id_23, info AS info_24 FROM movie_info_idx WHERE (((info IS NOT NULL) AND (info < '8.5')) AND ((movie_id IS NOT NULL) AND (info_type_id IS NOT NULL)))) AS t5 ON (t8.movie_id_17 = t5.movie_id_22) INNER JOIN (SELECT id AS id_9 FROM info_type WHERE (((info IS NOT NULL) AND (info = 'rating')) AND (id IS NOT NULL))) AS t4 ON (t4.id_9 = t5.info_type_id_23)) AS t9 INNER JOIN (SELECT movie_id AS movie_id_27, keyword_id AS keyword_id_28 FROM movie_keyword WHERE ((movie_id IS NOT NULL) AND (keyword_id IS NOT NULL))) AS t3 ON ((t3.movie_id_27 = t9.movie_id_17) AND (t3.movie_id_27 = t9.movie_id_22)) INNER JOIN (SELECT id AS id_11 FROM keyword WHERE (keyword IN ('murder','murder-in-title','blood','violence') AND (id IS NOT NULL))) AS t2 ON (t2.id_11 = t3.keyword_id_28)) AS t10 INNER JOIN (SELECT id AS id_29, title AS title_30, kind_id AS kind_id_32 FROM title WHERE (((production_year IS NOT NULL) AND (production_year > 2010)) AND ((id IS NOT NULL) AND (kind_id IS NOT NULL)))) AS t1 ON (((t1.id_29 = t10.movie_id_17) AND (t1.id_29 = t10.movie_id_27)) AND (t1.id_29 = t10.movie_id_22))) AS t11 INNER JOIN (SELECT id AS id_14 FROM kind_type WHERE (((kind IS NOT NULL) AND (kind = 'movie')) AND (id IS NOT NULL))) AS t0 ON (t0.id_14 = t11.kind_id_32)) AS t12

SELECT min(name_11) AS alternative_name, min(name_18) AS voiced_character_name, min(name_44) AS voicing_actress, min(title_55) AS american_movie FROM (SELECT t11.name_11, t11.name_18, t11.name_44, t0.title_55 FROM (SELECT t10.name_11, t10.movie_id_26, t10.name_18, t10.movie_id_39, t10.name_44 FROM (SELECT t9.name_11, t9.movie_id_26, t9.role_id_30, t9.name_18, t9.movie_id_39, t2.name_44 FROM (SELECT t8.person_id_10, t8.name_11, t8.person_id_25, t8.movie_id_26, t8.role_id_30, t8.name_18, t4.movie_id_39 FROM (SELECT t7.person_id_10, t7.name_11, t6.person_id_25, t6.movie_id_26, t6.role_id_30, t5.name_18 FROM (SELECT person_id AS person_id_10, name AS name_11 FROM aka_name WHERE (person_id IS NOT NULL)) AS t7 INNER JOIN (SELECT person_id AS person_id_25, movie_id AS movie_id_26, person_role_id AS person_role_id_27, role_id AS role_id_30 FROM cast_info WHERE (note IN ('(voice)','(voice: Japanese version)','(voice) (uncredited)','(voice: English version)') AND ((((person_id IS NOT NULL) AND (person_role_id IS NOT NULL)) AND (movie_id IS NOT NULL)) AND (role_id IS NOT NULL)))) AS t6 ON (t7.person_id_10 = t6.person_id_25) INNER JOIN (SELECT id AS id_17, name AS name_18 FROM char_name WHERE (id IS NOT NULL)) AS t5 ON (t5.id_17 = t6.person_role_id_27)) AS t8 INNER JOIN (SELECT movie_id AS movie_id_39, company_id AS company_id_40 FROM movie_companies WHERE ((movie_id IS NOT NULL) AND (company_id IS NOT NULL))) AS t4 ON (t8.movie_id_26 = t4.movie_id_39) INNER JOIN (SELECT id AS id_31 FROM company_name WHERE (((country_code IS NOT NULL) AND (country_code = '[us]')) AND (id IS NOT NULL))) AS t3 ON (t4.company_id_40 = t3.id_31)) AS t9 INNER JOIN (SELECT id AS id_43, name AS name_44 FROM name WHERE ((((gender IS NOT NULL) AND (name IS NOT NULL)) AND ((gender = 'f') AND (name LIKE '%An%'))) AND (id IS NOT NULL))) AS t2 ON ((t2.id_43 = t9.person_id_25) AND (t9.person_id_10 = t2.id_43))) AS t10 INNER JOIN (SELECT id AS id_52 FROM role_type WHERE (((role IS NOT NULL) AND (role = 'actress')) AND (id IS NOT NULL))) AS t1 ON (t10.role_id_30 = t1.id_52)) AS t11 INNER JOIN (SELECT id AS id_54, title AS title_55 FROM title WHERE (id IS NOT NULL)) AS t0 ON ((t11.movie_id_26 = t0.id_54) AND (t0.id_54 = t11.movie_id_39))) AS t12
